          <div class="articleAttrContent">
           <div class="articleAttrSection">
            <h3 style="text-align: center;">
             <span id="aHeadlineLabel" name="aHeadlineLabel">
              16 Simple Crochet Afghan Patterns
             </span>
            </h3>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             <a href="#Simple_Crochet_Afghan_Patterns">
              Simple Crochet Afghan Patterns
             </a>
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             <a href="#Simple Patterns for Striped Afghans">
              Simple Patterns for Striped Crochet Afghans
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Easy, simple, beginner - so many names for so many great afghans! These 16 simple crochet afghan patterns are perfect for anyone that loves to crochet but is short on time. These simple crochet patterns are also great for anyone looking for some extra practice. With a variety of pattern styles, you'll be able to find the simplest afghan for you to try in this collection. It's just that simple.
            </p>
            <p style="text-align: center;">
             <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="http://cf2.primecp.com/master_images/1-16 Simple.jpg" style="width: 500px; height: 357px; border-width: 0px; border-style: solid; margin: 5px;"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             Check out these great patterns and see all of the projects you can make in a short amount of time. From simple crochet afghans to easy crochet afghan patterns, we've got you covered. With the right hook, some great yarn and an imagination, you'll be on your way to making projects you can show to friends. No matter if you are an advanced crocheter or just starting out, these simple crochet patterns are great for crocheters of all skill levels.
            </p>
            <h2>
             <a name="Simple_Crochet_Afghan_Patterns">
              Simple Crochet Afghan Patterns
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Gingham-Ghan" target="_blank" title="Gingham Ghan">
              <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="http://cf2.primecp.com/master_images/AllFreeCrochetAfghanPatterns/Gingham-Ghan.jpg" style="width: 250px; height: 188px; border-width: 0px; border-style: solid; margin: 5px; float: right;"/>
             </a>
             These afghans are all easy and fun. Crochet should be a fun, relaxing experience - there's no point in stressing over difficult patterns. From baby blankets to granny squares, we've got the best quick and simple patterns out there! These afghan patterns are all about breaking down the fundamentals and laying down the foundation for a fantastic hobby. Whether you're new to crochet or just need a quick brush up on your skills, these patterns will have you hooked.
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Ripple/Classically-Simple-Shell" target="_blank" title="Classically Simple Shell">
               Classically Simple Shell
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Baby-Blanket-Afghans/Easy-Peasy-Worsted-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Easy Peasy Worsted Afghan">
               Easy Peasy Worsted Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Geometric/Neon-Lights-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Neon Lights Afghan">
               Neon Lights Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Motif-Afghans/Brick-Stitch-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Brick Stitch Afghan">
               Brick Stitch Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Throw-Patterns/Camouflage-Patch-Throw" target="_blank" title="Camouflage Patch Throw">
               Camouflage Patch Throw
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Granny-Square/Cottage-Relaxation-Granny-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Cottage Relaxation Granny Afghan">
               Cottage Relaxation Granny Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Geometric/Crochet-Circles-in-Squares-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Crochet Circles in Squares Afghan">
               Crochet Circles in Squares Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Gingham-Ghan" target="_blank" title="Gingham Ghan">
               Gingham Ghan
              </a>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
            </p>
            <h2>
             <a name="Simple Patterns for Striped Afghans">
              Simple Patterns for Striped Crochet Afghans
             </a>
            </h2>
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Beach-Stripe-Surf-Blanket" target="_blank" title="Beach Stripe Surf Blanket">
              <img alt="" itemprop="image" src="http://cf2.primecp.com/master_images/AllFreeCrochetAfghanPatterns/Beach-Stripe-Surf-Blanket.jpg" style="width: 250px; height: 224px; border-width: 0px; border-style: solid; margin: 5px; float: right;"/>
             </a>
             Simple afghans don't have to be boring - try some crochet stripes! With these simple patterns, you'll find that it's not hard to crochet a pattern with more than one color. Striped crochet patterns are nice because the stitch pattern always repeats so once you get started, you'll be able to even memorize some of these patterns. Simple crochet patterns will help you crochet quickly and these patterns will help you move on to more advanced patterns in the future.
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Beach-Stripe-Surf-Blanket" target="_blank" title="Beach Stripe Surf Blanket">
               Beach Stripe Surf Blanket
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Color-Burst-Granny-Stripes-Blanket" target="_blank" title="Color-Burst Granny Stripes Blanket">
               Color-Burst Granny Stripes Blanket
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Dots-and-Dashes-Throw" target="_blank" title="Dots and Dashes Throw">
               Dots and Dashes Throw
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Striped-Afghans/Lilac-Sound-Waves-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Lilac Sound-Waves Afghan">
               Lilac Sound-Waves Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Patterned-Afghans/Quick-as-a-Whip-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Quick as a Whip Afghan">
               Quick as a Whip Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Patterned-Afghans/No-Beginning-Chain-Bricks-Afghan" target="_blank" title="No Beginning Chain Bricks Afghan">
               No Beginning Chain Bricks Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Ripple/No-Beginning-Chain-Granny-Ripple-Afghan" target="_blank" title="No Beginning Chain Granny Ripple Blanket">
               No Beginning Chain Granny Ripple Blanket
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/Patterned-Afghans/Waves-of-Gray-Block-Afghan" target="_blank" title="Waves of Gray Afghan">
               Waves of Gray Afghan
              </a>
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
            </p>

   <div class="guidelinesText" style="display: none; position: absolute; margin: 0; padding: 15px; background-color: #fff; border: 5px solid #666;">
    <p style="text-align: right;">
     <a class="closeGuidelines" href="">
      close
     </a>
    </p>
    <h6 style="font-size: 1em;">
     Sharing Your Own Images
    </h6>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      Who can share images?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     You! Anyone who is a registered and logged in user.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      What should I share?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     Please share images that will help other visitors. For example:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Images that highlight a article's features ("Here are the controls on this music player", "See the clasp for this necklace", "Look at the box this came in")
     </li>
     <li>
      Images showing someone using a product ("Here I am wearing this scarf", "Install the ink cartridge here")
     </li>
     <li>
      Images related to a topic ("My dog Skipper", "A great outfit", "Our family at Yellowstone", "How to glue a chair using a cabinet clamp")
     </li>
     <li>
      Images that show how a product performs ("I took this picture with this camera", "This shirt shrunk in the wash", "The saw blade after 100 cuts")
     </li>
     <li>
      Images that give a sense of the size of the product ("This refrigerator is actually 6' tall", "A cellphone the size of a credit card")
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     Do include captions for your images. While not required, they provide context for your images.
					  Additionally, you can use the Image Notes feature to highlight one or more interesting areas in your image.  Everyone will see your notes when they roll over your image.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      What shouldn't I share?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     Behave as if you were a guest at a friend's dinner party: please treat the Prime Publishing community with respect. Do not share:
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Profane, obscene, or spiteful images, or any images with nudity
     </li>
     <li>
      Images to which you do not own the intellectual property rights
     </li>
     <li>
      Images featuring phone numbers, mail addresses, or URLs. You can watermark an image with copyright information.
     </li>
     <li>
      Images featuring availability, price, or alternative ordering/shipping information
     </li>
     <li>
      Images featuring external Web sites, contests, or other solicitations
     </li>
     <li>
      Any personal information about children under 13
     </li>
     <li>
      Images with automobile license plates that are prominent and easily read (pictures with license plates that have been fuzzed out or that otherwise cannot be read are acceptable).
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     The same guidelines apply to your captions and notes.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      What image formats and sizes are supported?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     We support JPEG, GIF and PNG images. Files must be no more than 1MB. Both the image height and the image width must be between 60 and 3500 pixels.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      Instead of uploading an image, can I just enter a link to an image?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     No, all images must be uploaded to Prime Publishing. This ensures your image is always available.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      How long does it take to upload an image?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     The time varies depending on the speed of your Internet connection and the size of the image file. For a 400KB image, for example, you should expect 2 to 4 minutes over a 56KB modem and under 1 minute for DSL or cable modem.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      Where will my image appear?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     Generally your image will appear where you uploaded it: in the article image gallery.
    </p>
    <p>
     <b class="h3">
      Who owns the images I upload?
     </b>
    </p>
    <p>
     The rights owner of the image continues to own the image; uploading your image to Prime Publishing does not transfer ownership.
    </p>
    <p style="text-align: right;">
     <a class="closeGuidelines" href="">
      close
     </a>
    </p>

     Company websites are not intended for use by individuals under the age of 18 or those who are not legal residents of the United States. By using our website or submitting information to us, you consent to the Company's use and sharing of the information collected or submitted as described in this Privacy Policy. If you are not 18 years of age or older and a valid resident of the United States or you do not agree with the terms of this Privacy Policy, do not provide us with any information or use any of the products or services offered or provided on Company websites or through Company technology.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      YOUR CALIFORNIA PRIVACY RIGHTS
     </strong>
     <br/>
     Beginning January 1, 2005 under California's "Shine the Light" law, California residents who provide personal information in obtaining products or services for personal, family or household use are entitled to either: (1) a list detailing the categories of information shared and the entities to which such information was provided; or (2) to be notified of a mechanism by which a consumer may opt-out of having their information shared with third parties. We have elected the second option. To opt-out of having your information shared with third parties please write to us.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      HOW DO WE COLLECT INFORMATION AND WHAT INFORMATION DO WE COLLECT?
     </strong>
     <br/>
     We collect and combine personally identifiable information ("PII") and non-personally identifiable information ("Non-PII") through various sources, including those discussed below. For your reference, PII is data collected with an intention to specifically identify, contact or locate a person, including but not limited to name, address, telephone number, or e-mail address. Conversely, Non-PII is data that is not used to specifically identify, contact or locate an individual, including but not limited to zip code, gender, age, or IP address.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Distribution Partners
     </strong>
     <br/>
     Website operators that license our ad serving technology pass information to us so that we may serve advertisements to you. The information passed may include, but is not limited to, your IP address, e-mail address, name, mailing address, telephone number, date of birth, and gender.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Offer Forms
     </strong>
     <br/>
     We also collect information about you when you complete a survey or offer form on one of our websites or web pages. This information may include, but is not limited to: your e-mail address, name, mailing address, telephone number, date of birth, gender, and payment information; information about your background, interests, health, education, career goals, and shopping preferences; and any other personal information or unique preference information you provide to us or our advertisers.
    </p>
    <p>

     </strong>

This information may include, but is not limited to: your IP address, e-mail address, name, mailing address, telephone number, date of birth, gender, and payment information; information about your background, interests, health, education, career goals, and shopping preferences; and any other information you provide to our website publisher partner.

A cookie is placed on your computer when your web browser accesses our website. We use cookies for tracking transactions and the user characteristics explained in detail throughout this Privacy Policy. If you choose, there are utilities available for purchase from independent software providers to install on your computer as well as tools/preferences you can choose through most web browsers to make website visits anonymous. Of course, cookies let you have a more satisfying website experience, so we recommend that you leave them turned on.

     We may serve advertisements to you based, in part, on your IP address, the demographic and geographic information you submitted to the Company during the website registration process, and other socio-economic information, psychographic information, Internet behavior (i.e., browsing, search, shopping, purchase, and ad response behavior), and lifestyle information about you that we obtain from affiliated entities and from third parties.
    </p>

These companies may use information (not including your name, address, email address or telephone number) about your visits to this and other websites in order to provide advertisements on our site, other websites and other forms of media about goods and services of interest to you. Additionally, this technology may pre-fill some or all of the offers' data fields with the information you submitted during the website registration process in order to prevent you from having to re-enter this information. We may not show all of the pre-filled data fields to you.
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      Upsell
     </strong>
     <br/>
     We utilize customized post transactional or "upsell" technology to help advertisers generate sales, while providing you with a series of great offers we think may be of interest to you. The way it works is simple: once you purchase a product or service from one of our reward advertisers, you will be offered additional products or services that we think may be of interest to you. If you elect to purchase products or services from an advertiser in the post transactional channel, we will pass the information that you provided during the initial transaction to the subsequent advertiser, including but not limited to your credit card information. This information pass is done to enhance and simplify your purchasing experience. Your information will only be passed to an advertiser in the post transactional channel after you have elected to purchase their product or service. By electing to purchase their product or service you consent to the passing of your data to the third party advertiser in question.
     <br/>
     <br/>

      Customer Service and Fulfillment
     </strong>
     <br/>
     We may use your information to operate the website promotion, service your account and to fulfill rewards earned through Company websites. We may also use your information to verify your identity or claimed account status and, where we consider appropriate, investigate your compliance with the terms and conditions of the website promotion or any advertiser offer. We do retain customer service correspondence.

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var facebook_login_obj = {};
			
			var FB;

			window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
			
				//console.log('call to window.fbAsyncInit line 20966');
			
				FB.init({
                    appId      : '375670195810722', // App ID Favecrafts
                    version    : 'v2.0',
					
					channelUrl : '//http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/channel.php', // Channel File
					status     : false, // check login status
					cookie     : true, // enable cookies to allow the server to access the session
					xfbml      : true  // parse XFBML
				});
				
				
				/*
				FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
					  if (response.status === 'connected') {
					    // connected
					    console.log('connected');
					  } else if (response.status === 'not_authorized') {
					    // not_authorized
					    console.log('not_authorized');
					  } else {
					    // not_logged_in
					    console.log('not_logged_in');
					  }
				});
				*/
				
				// listen for and handle auth.statusChange events
				FB.Event.subscribe(
					'auth.statusChange',
					function(response) {
						//alert('FB.Event.subscribe');
						//console.log('FB.Event.subscribe');
						
						facebook_login_obj.response = response;
						
						if (response.authResponse) {
							//alert('response.authResponse.accessToken:' + response.authResponse.accessToken);
							//console.log('response.authResponse.accessToken:' + response.authResponse.accessToken);
							
							// user has auth'd your app and is logged into Facebook
							FB.api(
								'/me', 
								function(me){
									facebook_login_obj.me = me;
									/*
									if (me.name) {
										document.getElementById('auth-displayname').innerHTML = me.name;
									}
									*/
									var alert_str = 'back from FB.api' + "\n\n";
									alert_str += 'me: ' + me + "\n\n";
   									alert_str += 'me.name: ' + me.name + "\n\n";
   									alert_str += 'me.email: ' + me.email + "\n\n";
   									alert_str += 'me.error_code: ' + me.error_code + "\n\n";
   									alert_str += 'me.error_msg: ' + me.error_msg + "\n\n";
   									//alert(alert_str);
   									
   									
   									//maybe look for error_code??
   									facebook_login_obj.loginToPrimeViaFb();
								}
							);
							//document.getElementById('auth-loggedout').style.display = 'none';
							//document.getElementById('auth-loggedin').style.display = 'block';
							
							
						} else {
							// user has not auth'd your app, or is not logged into Facebook
							//document.getElementById('auth-loggedout').style.display = 'block';
							//document.getElementById('auth-loggedin').style.display = 'none';
						}
						
					}
				);
		
				/*
				// respond to clicks on the login and logout links

				  FB.login();
				});
				document.getElementById('auth-logoutlink').addEventListener('click', function(){
				  FB.logout();
				}); 
				*/
			  
			};
		  
			// Load the SDK Asynchronously
			(function(d){
			   var js, id = 'facebook-jssdk', ref = d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
			   if (d.getElementById(id)) {return;}
			   js = d.createElement('script');
			   js.id = id;
			   js.async = true;
			   js.src = "//connect.facebook.net/en_US/sdk.js";
			   ref.parentNode.insertBefore(js, ref);
			}(document));
			
			
			facebook_login_obj.loginToPrimeViaFb = function(){
				var alert_str = 'facebook_login_obj.loginToPrimeViaFb' + "\n";
				alert_str += 'facebook_login_obj.response.authResponse.accessToken: ' + facebook_login_obj.response.authResponse.accessToken + "\n";
				alert_str += 'facebook_login_obj.me.email: ' + facebook_login_obj.me.email + "\n";
				//alert(alert_str);
				
				if(
					facebook_login_obj.response.authResponse.accessToken != undefined  &amp;&amp;
					facebook_login_obj.me.email != undefined
				){

                // get the profile picture    
                    FB.api(
                        '/me/picture', 
                        function(resp){
                            facebook_login_obj.profile_url = resp.data.url;
        
                            $.ajax({
                                url: "/ajax_process.php",
                                type: 'GET',
                                cache: false,
                                dataType: "json",
                                timeout: 10000,
                                data: {
                                    task: 'fb_user_acct_login',
                                    email: facebook_login_obj.me.email,
                                    fname: facebook_login_obj.me.first_name,
                                    lname: facebook_login_obj.me.last_name,
                                    profile_url: facebook_login_obj.profile_url,
                                    fb_user_id: facebook_login_obj.me.id,
                                    access_token: facebook_login_obj.response.authResponse.accessToken
                                },
                                complete: function(){
                                    
                                },
                                success: function(json){
                                    //alert('loginToPrimeViaFb success');
                                    if(json.success == 1){
                                        $('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('You are logged in.');
                                        if( 1 ){
                                            setTimeout('location.reload(true)', 700);
                                        }
                                    }else{
                                        $('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('We could not log you in.');
                                        $('.dhtmlLoginWrapper .facebookLoginButton').fadeTo('normal', 1.0);
                                    }
                                    
                                    
                                    
                                }
                            });

                        }
                    );

				}else{
					//alert('We are sorry. There was an issue attempting to log you in with Facebook');
					$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('We are sorry. There was an issue attempting to log you in with Facebook');
					$('.dhtmlLoginWrapper .facebookLoginButton').fadeTo('normal', 1.0);
				}

			}
  </script>

  <!-- START Google Authentication js -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   // Defines the configuration options, these must be set before you load
			// the plusone.js file.
			/*
			window.___gcfg = {
				lang: 'en-US',
				parsetags: 'explicit',
			}
			*/
			
			//var gapi;
			
			var google_login_obj = {};
			google_login_obj.js_loaded = false;
			google_login_obj.init_limit = 10;
			google_login_obj.init_attempt = 0;

			// just our div id wrapping theirs
			google_login_obj.googleLoginButtonID = 'googleLoginButton';
			google_login_obj.token;
			google_login_obj.user = {};
			
			
			
			$(document).ready(
				function() {
				
					google_login_obj.init();
					
				}
			);
			
			
			google_login_obj.init = function(){
				//console.log('google_login_obj.init');
				google_login_obj.init_attempt++;
				if(google_api_obj.loaded == true){
					google_login_renderButton();
				}else{
					if(google_login_obj.init_attempt &lt; google_login_obj.init_limit){
						setTimeout('google_login_obj.init()', 1000);
					}
				}
			}
			
			
			
			// loads the google js file for the signin
			/*
			google_login_obj.loadGoogleJs = function(){
				console.log('google_login_obj.loadGoogleJs for LOGIN');
				
					var po = document.createElement('script');
					po.type = 'text/javascript';
					po.async = true;
					po.src = 'https://apis.google.com/js/client:plusone.js?onload=google_login_loaded';
					var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
					s.parentNode.insertBefore(po, s);
			}
			*/
			
			
			function google_login_loaded(){
				//console.log('google_login_loaded called in getJavascript_loadGoogleAuthentication');
				google_login_obj.js_loaded = true;
				google_login_renderButton();
			}
			
			
			/*
			this is the call back function that runs when the user triggers the google log in
			would not work as an obj prop, only a function
			*/
			google_login_signinCallback = function(authResult){
				//console.log('google_login_signinCallback');
				//console.log(authResult);
				google_login_obj.authResult = authResult;
				
				
				if(authResult['access_token']){
					// Successfully authorized
					//console.log('login worked');
					google_login_obj.token = gapi.auth.getToken();
					//console.log('access_token: ' + google_login_obj.token.access_token);
					//console.log('id_token: ' + google_login_obj.token.id_token);
					
					
					google_login_obj.showWaiting();
					google_login_obj.getUserEmail(1);
					
					
				}else if(authResult['error']){
					// There was an error.
					// Possible error codes:
					//   "access_denied" - User denied access to your app
					//   "immediate_failed" - Could not automatically log in the user
					//console.log('There was an error: ' + authResult['error']);
				}
			}
			
			
			google_login_obj.getUserName = function() {
				gapi.client.load(
					'plus', 
					'v1', 
					function() {
						var request = gapi.client.plus.people.get(
							{
								'userId': 'me'
							}
						);
						request.execute(
							function(resp) {
								//console.log(resp);
								//console.log('f name: ' + resp.name.givenName);
								//console.log('l name: ' + resp.name.familyName);
								google_login_obj.user.first_name = resp.name.givenName;
								google_login_obj.user.last_name = resp.name.familyName;
							}
						);
					}
				);
			}
	      
			// get the user's email, with an optional param to call the prime login when retrieved
			google_login_obj.getUserEmail = function(call_login) {
				gapi.client.load(
					'oauth2', 
					'v2', 
					function() {
						gapi.client.oauth2.userinfo.get().execute(
							function(resp) {
								// Shows user email
								//console.log(resp.email);
								google_login_obj.user.email = resp.email;
								if(call_login){
									google_login_obj.loginToPrime();
								}
							}
						)
					}
				);
				
			}
	      
			google_login_obj.loginToPrime = function(){
				//console.log('loginToPrime');
				//console.log(google_login_obj.user);
				
				$.ajax({
					url: "/ajax_process.php",
					type: 'GET',
					cache: false,
					dataType: "json",
					timeout: 10000,
					data: {
						task: 'google_user_acct_login',
						email: google_login_obj.user.email,
						fname: google_login_obj.user.first_name,
						lname: google_login_obj.user.last_name,
						access_token: google_login_obj.token.access_token
					},
					complete: function(){
						
					},
					success: function(json){
						//alert('loginToPrimeViaFb success');
						google_login_obj.clearWaiting();
						if(json.success == 1){
							$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('You are logged in.');
							if( 1 ){
								setTimeout('location.reload(true)', 700);
							}
						}else{
							$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('We could not log you in.');
						}
					}
				});
					
				
				
			} // end google_login_obj.loginToPrime
			
			
			
			google_login_obj.showWaiting = function(){
				$('#' + google_login_obj.googleLoginButtonID).fadeTo('normal', 0.3);
				$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('&lt;img src="/images/ajax-loader-bar.gif" alt="Loading" width="220" height="19" /&gt;');
			}
			
			google_login_obj.clearWaiting = function(){
				$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('');
				$('#' + google_login_obj.googleLoginButtonID).fadeTo('normal', 1.0);
			}
			
			
			
			
			
			// called once the google js is loaded
			function google_login_renderButton(){
				//console.log('google_login_renderButton');
				
				if(gapi != undefined){
					//console.log('gapi exists');
					gapi.signin.render(
						google_login_obj.googleLoginButtonID,
						{
							'callback': 'google_login_signinCallback',
							'clientid': '1092413815831.apps.googleusercontent.com',
							'cookiepolicy': 'single_host_origin',
							//'requestvisibleactions': 'http://schemas.google.com/AddActivity', commented out 2014-05-22
							'approvalprompt': 'force',
							//'scope': 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/plus.login'
							//'scope': 'https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/userinfo'
							'scope': 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/userinfo.email'
							//'scope': 'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/email'
						}
					);
				}else{
					//console.log('gapi does not exist');
				}
				
			}
			// https://developers.google.com/+/api/oauth#login-scopes
			// http://stackoverflow.com/questions/18489695/disable-automatic-authentication-for-google-social-sign-in/18494814#18494814
  </script>
  <!-- END Google Authentication js -->

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var twitter_login_obj = {};
			twitter_login_obj.loginButtonClass = 'twitterLoginButton';
			twitter_login_obj.window_ref;
			twitter_login_obj.window_name = 'twitter_login_window';
			
			twitter_login_obj.window_width = 700;
			twitter_login_obj.window_features = 'menubar=yes,location=yes,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,status=yes,width=' + twitter_login_obj.window_width + ',height=500,top=200,left=';
			
			
			$(document).ready(
				function() {
					//console.log('getJavascript_loadTwitterAuthentication');
					twitter_login_obj.init();
					
					var width = $(window).width();
					var left = ( width - twitter_login_obj.window_width ) / 2;
					twitter_login_obj.window_features += left;
				}
			);
			
			twitter_login_obj.init = function(){
				$('.' + twitter_login_obj.loginButtonClass).click(
					function(){
						//console.log(twitter_login_obj.loginButtonClass + ' click');
						twitter_login_obj.openWindow();			
					}
				);
			}
			
			
			twitter_login_obj.openWindow = function(){
				twitter_login_obj.window_ref = window.open("/login_with_twitter.php", twitter_login_obj.window_name, twitter_login_obj.window_features);
			}
			
			twitter_login_obj.requestCanceled = function(){
				//console.log('twitter_login_obj.requestCanceled');

				setTimeout("$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('');", 5000);
			}
			
			twitter_login_obj.loginSuccessful = function(){
				$('#dhtmlLogin .feedbackDiv').html('You are logged in.');
				if( 1 ){
					setTimeout('location.reload(true)', 700);
				}
			}
  </script>

  <!-- START newsletter js -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var signup_redirect_qry_params = new Array();
        signup_redirect_qry_params['email'] = false;


        var signup_redirect_url = 'http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com/flow.php?grp=4';
        // 2014-04-08 we need the flows id
        var signup_redirect_id = '403';

                    var nscID = false;
            
                    var is_mustang = 0;
            
        /*
        this is an object that holds properties used to determine actions after the user signs up
        */
        var post_newsletter_signup = new Object();
        post_newsletter_signup.rediect_delay = 0;	// how long before we redirect the user
        post_newsletter_signup.link_has_confirmation_pixel = 0;	// do we load an external confirmation pixel
        post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup = 0;

        var desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj = {};
        desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node;
        desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.default_input_text_str = '';
        desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout = '0';
        desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.page_loads = 1;


        $(document).ready( function() {
            function ajaxFormPreSubmit() {
                
                $('#newsletterSignUpLoader').show();
                
                // disable form fields
                //$("#fname").attr("disabled", true);
                //$("#lname").attr("disabled", true);
                $("#email").attr("disabled", true);
                $("#signUpSubmit").attr("disabled", true);
                
                
                $('#newsletterSignUpForm').fadeTo("slow", 0.2);
                
                return true;
            }
            
            //pre-submit for dhtml
            function ajaxFormPreSubmit2() {
                
                //$('#newsletterSignUpLoader2').show();
                
                //$('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI').fadeTo("slow", 0.2);
                // #newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI is for standard desktop
                // #newsletterSignUpDivAnime input is for mobile dhtml on a desktop
                $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI, #newsletterSignUpDivAnime input').css(
                    {
                        'opacity': 0.3
                    }
                );
                
                // mobile
                $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .userFeedback_waiting').show();
                
                
                return true;
            }

            // set the onclick for the right rail newsletter sign up email text field
            $('#newsletterSignUpForm #email').click( 
                function () {
                
                    // this removes the default text that appears in the text field
                    $('#newsletterSignUpForm #email').val('');	
                    
                    if ($(this).hasClass('defaultTextFieldColor')) {
                        // remove the class that sets the text color to grey
                        $(this).removeClass('defaultTextFieldColor');
                        // remove the default text
                        $(this).val('');
                    }
                }
                
            );
            
            
            // newsletter signup form - right column
            $('#newsletterSignUpForm').ajaxForm(
                {
                    beforeSubmit: ajaxFormPreSubmit,
                    success: function(response) {
                        
                        // log all submits, passing something about the success/new user
                        post_newsletter_signup.logRightRailSubmit(response.is_new_signup, $('#newsletterSignUpForm :input[name=rriID]').val());
                        
                        
                        //alert('result = ' + response.result);
                        
                        $('#newsletterSignUpLoader').hide();
                        
                        if (response.result &gt; 0) {
                            
                            // the user is signed up
                            
                            triggerWiderFunnel();
                            
                            // hide the sign up form fields
                            $('#newsletterSignUpForm').hide();
                            
                            // display thanks
                            $('#newsletterSignUpThanks').show();
                            
                            
                            // set a cookie so we know this user signed up
                            var alert_str = 'COOKIE_NAME_NL_SIGNUP = nlsignup' + "\n";
                            alert_str += 'COOKIE_EXP_DAYS_NL_SIGNUP = 1825' + "\n";
                            //alert(alert_str);
                            createCookie('nlsignup', 1825, 1825);
                            
                            
                            signup_redirect_qry_params['email'] = response.email;
                            
                            //setTimeout('signupRedirect()', 2000);
                            post_newsletter_signup.rediect_delay = 2000;
                            post_newsletter_signup.link_has_confirmation_pixel = response.fire_pixel;
                            post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup = response.is_new_signup; // right rail
                            postNewsletterSignup();
                            
                        } else {
                            // display error
                            //alert('response.result = ' + response.result);
                            
                            $('#newsletterSignUpError').show();
                            setTimeout("$('#newsletterSignUpError').hide()", 5000);
                            
                            $('#newsletterSignUpForm').fadeTo("slow", 1);
                            
                            // disable form fields
                            $("#fname").attr("disabled", false);
                            $("#lname").attr("disabled", false);
                            $("#email").attr("disabled", false);
                            $("#signUpSubmit").attr("disabled", false);
                            
                            //alert('Sorry, we could not sign you up.');
                        }
                        
                        

                        
                        
                        
                        
                        
                        //alert('newsletterSignUpForm success ' + response.lname);
                        
                        //alert($("#lname").attr("disabled"););
                    },
                    dataType: 'json'
                }
            );

            
            
            
            
            $("#newsletterSignUpDivAnimeCloseLink").click(
                function() {
                    // the user closed the window w/o signing up
                    // plant a cookie so the signup does not appear for this session
                    //setNlSignUpCookie();
                    createCookie('nlsignup', 1, 0);
                    
                    hideNewsletterSignUpFormAnime();
                    
                    return false;
                }
            );
            
            
            /**
             *if the newsletter signup form has an input with name 'move_privacy'
             *get the value of that hidden input. it is the id of the html element where we will move the privacy link
             *append the existing link to the new html element
             */
            if($('#newsletterSignUpFormAnime input[name=move_privacy]').val()){
                var new_id = $('#newsletterSignUpFormAnime input[name=move_privacy]').val();
                $('#' + new_id).append($('#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink a'));
                
                $('#' + new_id + ' a').click(
                    function() {
                        
                        return displayDhtmlPrivacyPolicy();
                    }
                );
            }
            
            
            /**
            *2013-11-14
            *#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink is from the "standard / older" desktop dhtml
            * .newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink is from 'newer / "mobile" ' dhtml and uses a class
            *we are replacing lots of jq selects, xxx, with a var holding the link
            *this solves the issue where some versions use an ID and some use a CLASS
            *we testing for the class version first, I only want to find one, not both. 
            *a mobile version on desktop will have both
            *we might need a better way to do this at somepoint, but it works today
            */
            desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node = $("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink, .newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink");
            
            if ($(".newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink").length ) {
                desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node = $(".newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink");
            }else if ($("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink").length ) {
                desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node = $("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink");
            }
            
            
            //$("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink a, .newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink a").click(
            $(desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node).find('a').click(
                function() {
                    //alert('click privacy link');
                    //return false;
                    
                    return displayDhtmlPrivacyPolicy();
                }
            );
            
            // set the behavior of the close links in the privacy div
            $('#newsletterSignUpPrivacyContent a.closePrivacyContentLink').click(
                function () {
                    
                    //alert('newsletterSignUpPrivacyContent a.closePrivacyContentLink');
                    
                    // fade in the signup form content
                    $('#newsletterSignUpAnimeContent').fadeTo('slow', 1.0);
                    
                    // show the link that opens the privacy content
                    //$("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink").show();
                    $(desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.privacy_link_div_node).show();
                    
                    // show the link that closes the dhtml content
                    $("#newsletterSignUpDivAnimeCloseLink").show();
                    
                    
                    // hide the privacy content
                    $('#newsletterSignUpPrivacyContent').hide();
                    
                    return false;
                }
            );
            
            
            
            
            // when the user clicks the text field, blank any default value
            //$("#newsletterSignUpFormAnime #emailAnime").focus(	// this selector is for the standard / desktop version
            $("#newsletterSignUpFormAnime input[name=email]").focus(	// this selector handles the standard / desktop version and a moble version used on the desktop
                function(){
                    $(this).val('');
                }
            );
            
            
            
            
            // newsletter signup form - dhtml
            $('#newsletterSignUpFormAnime').ajaxForm(
                {
                    beforeSubmit: ajaxFormPreSubmit2,
                    success: function(response) {
                        
                        //alert('newsletterSignUpFormAnime result = ' + response.result);
                        
                        //$('#newsletterSignUpLoader2').hide();
                        
                        // mobile
                        $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .userFeedback_waiting').hide();
                        
                        if (response.result &gt; 0) {
                            
                            // the user is signed up
                            
                            triggerWiderFunnel();
                            
                            // hide the sign up form fields
                            $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI').hide();
                            
                            // display thanks
                            $('#newsletterSignUpThanksAnime').show();
                            
                            // mobile
                            $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .userFeedback_suucess').show();
                            
                            
                            // set a cookie so we know this user signed up
                            var alert_str = 'COOKIE_NAME_NL_SIGNUP = nlsignup' + "\n";
                            alert_str += 'COOKIE_EXP_DAYS_NL_SIGNUP = 1825' + "\n";
                            //alert(alert_str);
                            createCookie('nlsignup', 1825, 1825);
                            
                            signup_redirect_qry_params['email'] = response.email;
                            
                            
                            post_newsletter_signup.link_has_confirmation_pixel = response.fire_pixel;
                            post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup = response.is_new_signup; // main dhtml signup
                            
                            postNewsletterSignup();
                            
                            
                        } else {
                            // display error
                            //alert('response.result = ' + response.result);
                            
                            /**
                             *2010-2-11
                             *we have different types of dhtml signup forms
                             *some have a hidden input field to let us know how to behave here
                             */
                            switch($('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime input[name=dhtml_type]').val()){
                                case 'wider_funnel':
                                    
                                    //$('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI').fadeTo("fast", 1);
                                    $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI, #newsletterSignUpDivAnime input').css(
                                        {
                                            'opacity': 1.0
                                        }
                                    );
                                    
                                    $('#newsletterSignUpErrorAnime').show();
                                    
                                    switch(nscID){
                                        case 20:	// wider funnel A
                                            /**
                                             *change the position of a background image
                                             */
                                            $('#nscID_20 .errorDiv').css(
                                                {
                                                    'background-position' : '50% 0px'
                                                }
                                            );
                                            break;
                                        case 21:	// wider funnel B
                                            /**
                                             *change the background image
                                             */
                                            $('#nscID_21 .layoutTable tr.row2 td.td2').css(
                                                {
                                                    'background-image' : 'url(/site_templates/signup_creative/images/nscID_21/favecrafts_popup_varB_patterns_08-error.png)'
                                                }
                                            );
                                            break;
                                        case 22:	// wider funnel B
                                            /**
                                             *change the background image
                                             */
                                            $('#nscID_22 .layoutTable tr.row2 td.td2').css(
                                                {
                                                    'background-image' : 'url(/site_templates/signup_creative/images/nscID_22/favecrafts_popup_varC_community_07-error.png)'
                                                }
                                            );
                                            break;
                                        case 23:	// wider funnel D
                                            /**
                                             *change the position of a background image
                                             */
                                            $('#nscID_23 .errorDiv').css(
                                                {
                                                    'background-position' : '285px 8px'
                                                }
                                            );
                                            break;
                                    } // end nscID switch
                                    
                                    
                                    break; // end wider_funnel case
                                
                                default:
                                    // hide the sign up form fields
                                    $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .newsletterSignUpDivAnimeFormUI').hide();
                                    
                                    $('#newsletterSignUpErrorAnime').show();
                                    
                                    // mobile
                                    $('#newsletterSignUpDivAnime .userFeedback_error').show();
                                    
                                    setTimeout('hideNewsletterSignUpErrorAnime()', 3500);
                            }
                        }
                        
                    },
                    dataType: 'json'		
                }
            ); /// end the code that hijacks the signup anime div


        }); // end ready;
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function bookmark(url,title) {
            //alert('url = ' + url + "\n title = " + title);

            if (window.sidebar &amp;&amp; window.sidebar.addPanel) { // Mozilla Firefox Bookmark
                window.sidebar.addPanel(title, url, '');
                
            } else if(window.external &amp;&amp; ('AddFavorite' in window.external)) { // IE Favorite
                window.external.AddFavorite(url, title); 

            } else if(window.opera &amp;&amp; window.print) { // Opera Hotlist
                this.title=title;
                return true;

            } else { // webkit - safari/chrome
                $('#bookmarkDivAnime #bookmarkText').text((navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('mac') != - 1 ? 'Command/Cmd' : 'CTRL') + "+D");
                var doc_width = $(document).width();
                var doc_height = $(document).height();

                var popup_width = $("#bookmarkDivAnime").width();

                var popup_left = 0;
                if (popup_width &lt; doc_width) {
                    popup_left = (doc_width - popup_width) / 2;
                }

                $("#bookmarkDivAnime").css("position", "fixed");
                $("#bookmarkDivAnime").css("top", '-600px');
                $("#bookmarkDivAnime").css("left", popup_left + 'px');
                $("#bookmarkDivAnime").show();

                $("#bookmarkDivAnime").animate(
                    {"bottom": "100px"}, 
                    "slow",
                    '',
                    function () {
                        // this fires after the popup is in place
                        // fade out the div that will be placed over the page
                        // the div is not visible at this point, but we use fade out so we can fade it in after the css updates are made

                        $('#viewportGreyout').fadeTo(
                            "fast", 
                            0.0,
                            function () {
                                // set some css for the div then fade it in
                                $('#viewportGreyout').css( {
                                    position: 'absolute',
                                    margin: 0,
                                    padding: 0,
                                    'z-index': 500,
                                    'top' : '0',
                                    'left' : '0',
                                    'width' : doc_width + 'px',
                                    'height' : doc_height + 'px',
                                    'background-color' : '#000'
                                }).fadeTo("slow", 0.8).click(function(){
                                    /*
                                    2014-06-23
                                    clicking the greyout closes the dhtml, as if you clicked the close link/button
                                    */
                                    //console.log('click the greyport');
                                    //console.log('desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout: ' + desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout);
                                    if(desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout &gt; 0){
                                        $("#bookmarkDivAnimeCloseLink").click();
                                    }
                                });
                            }
                        );
                    }
                );
            }

            return false;
        }
  </script>

						(function() {

							window.PinIt = window.PinIt || { loaded:false };
							if (window.PinIt.loaded) return;
							window.PinIt.loaded = true;
							function async_load(){
								//console.log('async_load 123');
								var s = document.createElement("script");
								s.type = "text/javascript";
								s.setAttribute('data-pin-hover', true); // 2013-08-24 - pinit image hover feature
								s.async = true;
								s.src = "http://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js";
								var x = document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];
								x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x);
							}
							if (window.attachEvent){
								window.attachEvent("onload", async_load);
							}else{
								window.addEventListener("load", async_load, false);
							}
						})();
						
						
					//} // end main func

  <!-- js array x = 3 -->
  <script>
   $(function() {
            // The element that is fluid width
            var $fluidEl = $("#col2");
            var $iframeVideos = $("iframe[src^='//www.youtube.com']");
            var $objectVideos  = $("object, embed");

            resizeVideos($iframeVideos, 'iframe');
            //resizeVideos($objectVideos, 'object');


            function resizeVideos( videos, method ) {
                // Figure out and save aspect ratio for each video
                videos.each(function() {
                    if ( method === "iframe" ) {
                        $(this).data('aspectRatio', this.height / this.width);
                    } else {
                        // cant assign data to an OBJECT tag
                        $(this).attr('data-aspectRatio', this.height / this.width);

                    }

                    $(this)
                        // and remove the hard coded width/height
                        .removeAttr('height')
                        .removeAttr('width');
                });

                // When the window is resized
                $(window).resize(function() {
                    var newWidth = $fluidEl.width();

                    
                    // Resize all videos according to their own aspect ratio
                    videos.each(function() {
                        var $el = $(this);
                        $el.width(newWidth);
                        
                        if ( method === "iframe" ) {
                            $el.height(newWidth * $el.data('aspectRatio'));
                        } else {
                            $el.height(newWidth * $el.attr('data-aspectRatio'));
                        }

                    });

                // Kick off one resize to fix all videos on page load
                }).resize();

            }
        });
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var pdf_download_obj = new Object();
			pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in = false;
			pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie = false;

			pdf_download_obj.link_href = '';
			pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error = false;
			pdf_download_obj.page_title = '';
							pdf_download_obj.page_title = "16 Simple Crochet Afghan Patterns";
							
		
			$(document).ready(
				function() {
				
					if(pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in  ||  pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie){
						pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download = false;
					}
				
					var alert_str = 'getJavascript_pdfDownload ready line: 14928' + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in: ' + pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie: ' + pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download: ' + pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.page_title: ' + pdf_download_obj.page_title + "\n";
					//alert(alert_str);
					//console.log(alert_str);
					
					// 2013-07-02
					// event tracking
					// new click event we always do
					$('a.launchPdfDownloadDhtml').click(
						function(){
							// event tracking
							//console.log('start event tracking');
							//onClick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Download', 'eBook', '{Dynamically insert Title here}',, false]);"
							
							ga(
                                'send', 
                                'event', 
                                'Download', 
                                'eBook', 
                                pdf_download_obj.page_title
							);
							//console.log('end event tracking');
						}
					);
					
					
					/**
					*as the page loads, if the pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download flag true
					*additional click events we may do
					*/
					if(pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download){
					
						pdf_download_obj.initDhtml();
						
						$('a.launchPdfDownloadDhtml').click(
							function(){
								var return_value = false;
	
								var alert_str = 'pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in: ' + pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in + "\n";
								alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie: ' + pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie + "\n";
								alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download: ' + pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download + "\n";
								//alert(alert_str);
								//console.log(alert_str);
						
								//var click_return = true;
								//alert( $(this).attr('href') );
								pdf_download_obj.link_href = $(this).attr('href');
								var link_arr = pdf_download_obj.link_href.split('=');
								
								/**
								*does the format of the href meet our expectations
								*/
								if(link_arr.length &gt; 1){
									//alert(link_arr[1]);
									pdf_download_obj.pdf_id = link_arr[1];
									
									alert_str = 'pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in: ' + pdf_download_obj.user_logged_in + "\n";
									alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie: ' + pdf_download_obj.has_signup_cookie + "\n";
									alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download: ' + pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download + "\n";
									alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.pdf_id: ' + pdf_download_obj.pdf_id + "\n";
									//alert(alert_str);
									
									/**
									*now the user is actually clicking a link
									*make sure the pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download flag is still true
									*/
									if(pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download){
										pdf_download_obj.displaySignup();	
									}else{
										return_value = true;
									}
									
									
									
								}else{
									alert('Sorry. We cannot find this file.');
									//click_return = false;
								}
								
								
								return return_value;
							}
						);
					}
				}
			);
			
			pdf_download_obj.initDhtml = function(){
				//alert('pdf_download_obj.initDhtml');
				
				$('body').append('&lt;div id="' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + '" class="dhtmlLoginWrapper" style="display: none;"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
				
			}
			
			pdf_download_obj.displaySignup = function(){
				//alert('pdf_download_obj.displaySignup');
				
				$.ajax({
					url: "/ajax_process.php",
					type: 'GET',
					cache: false,
					dataType: "html",
					timeout: 10000,
					data: (
						{
							task: 'get_pdf_download_pdf_dhtml',
							pdfID: pdf_download_obj.pdf_id
						}
					),
					complete: function(){
						//$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id).center().slideDown();
					},
					success: function(html){
					
						pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error = false;
					
						if(html == 'no-data'){
							/**
							*for whatever reason, we have no content to show
							*allow the user to download the file
							*/
							pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error = true;
							pdf_download_obj.closeDhtml();
						}else{
							/**
							* add the dhtml we got back to the page and set some css
							*/
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id).html(html).css(
								{
									'width' : '600px',
									'margin' : '0px',
									'padding' : '5px',
									'background-color' : '#fff',
									'border' : '5px solid #333'
								}
							);
							
							
							pdf_download_obj.hijackForm();
							
							
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .privacyPolicyLink').click(
								function(){
									//alert('click privacyPolicyLink');
									
									$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .privacyContent').slideDown();
									
									return false;
								}
							).hover(
								function(){
									$(this).css(
										{
											'color' : '#000',
										}
									);
								},
								function(){
									$(this).css(
										{
											'color' : '#a9a9a9'
										}
									);
								}
							);
							
							
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .closePrivacyContentLink').click(
								function(){
									$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .privacyContent').slideUp();
									
									return false;
								}
							);
							
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .closeBoxText').hover(
								function(){
									$(this).css(
										{
											'color' : '#000',
											'cursor' : 'pointer'
										}
									);
								},
								function(){
									$(this).css(
										{
											'color' : '#666'
										}
									);
								}
							);
							
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .closeBox').click(
								function(){
									//alert('click close box');
									pdf_download_obj.closeDhtml();
								}
							);
							
							
							/**
							*set some behavior for the email text field 
							*/
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' form input[name=email]').val('Enter your email address').click(
								function(){
									$(this).select();
									if($(this).val() == 'Enter your email address'){
										$(this).val('');
									}
								}
							);
							
							$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id).center().slideDown();
						}
					}
				});
				
				pdf_download_obj.closeDhtml = function(){
					var alert_str = 'pdf_download_obj.closeDhtml' + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.link_href: ' + pdf_download_obj.link_href + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error: ' + pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error + "\n";
					alert_str += 'pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download: ' + pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download + "\n";
					
					//alert(alert_str);
								
					$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id).slideUp();
					
					window.location = pdf_download_obj.link_href;
					//alert(pdf_download_obj.link_href);
					
					/**
					*as long as there was not some issue getting the popup content, we will turn off the pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download flag
					*/
					if(pdf_download_obj.popup_content_error == false){
						/**
						*some action by the user got us here where we are closing the dhtml and starting a download
						*update this property so the user can click other links on the page and download w/o popup
						*/
						pdf_download_obj.show_signup_before_download = false;
					}
				}
				
				pdf_download_obj.hijackForm = function(){
					//alert('pdf_download_obj.hijackForm');
					//console.log('pdf_download_obj.hijackForm');
					
					$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' form').ajaxForm(
						{
							beforeSubmit: pdf_download_obj.ajaxFormPreSubmit,
							dataType: 'json',
							success: function(json) {

								var alert_str = 'getJavascript_newsletterSignupPage success' + "\n";
								alert_str += 'json.result: ' + json.result + "\n";
								alert_str += 'json.fname: ' + json.fname + "\n";
								alert_str += 'json.lname: ' + json.lname + "\n";
								alert_str += 'json.phone: ' + json.phone + "\n";
								alert_str += 'json.email: ' + json.email + "\n";
								
								//alert(alert_str);
								
								if (json.result &gt; 0) {
									//$('#newsletterSignupPageDiv fieldset').hide();
									//$('#newsletterSignupPageDiv .formSuccess').show();
									
									createCookie('nlsignup', 1825, 1825);
									
									
									$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .userFeedback').html('Your download will begin shortly.&lt;br /&gt;Or &lt;a href="' + pdf_download_obj.link_href + '"&gt;click here&lt;/a&gt; to download your file.');
									
									setTimeout("pdf_download_obj.closeDhtml()", 1000);
									
								} else {
									var alert_str = 'We could not sign you up.' + "\n";
									alert_str += 'Please review the information you entered and make sure your email address is correct.' + "\n";
									
									//alert(alert_str);
									
									$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' .userFeedback').html('We could not sign you up.&lt;br /&gt;Please check your email address and try again.');
								
									$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' form').fadeTo("slow", 1.0);	
								}
								
								
							} // end success
						}
					);
				}
				
				pdf_download_obj.ajaxFormPreSubmit = function() {
					var alert_str = 'pdf_download_obj.ajaxFormPreSubmit' + "\n";
					//alert(alert_str);
					
					var result = true;
					
					var email_val = $('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' form input[name=email]').val();
					
					if(
						email_val == ''  ||
						email_val == 'Enter your email address'  ||
						email_val.search("Enter your email address") &gt;= 0
					) {
						result = false;
						alert('You must enter a valid email address.');
					}
					
					
					if (result == true) {
						$('#' + pdf_download_obj.dhtml_signup_id + ' form').fadeTo("slow", .3);	
					}
					
					
					return result;
				}
			}

			function initPrivateNote(html){
				/**
				*add the note text to the html version
			   */
			   $(".privateNoteText span").html(html);
			   
			   /**
				*add the note text to the text area
			   */
			   $("#mynotes").val(html);
					
				if(html != ''){
					private_note.text = html;
				}else{
					private_note.text = false;
				}
			}
			
			function toggleNoteContent(){
				//console.log('toggleNoteContent');
				//console.log('private_note.form_displayed: ' + private_note.form_displayed);
				
				if(private_note.form_displayed == true){
					
					$('#privateNoteForm').slideUp('slow');
					private_note.form_displayed = false;
					
					if(private_note.text != false){
						/**
						 *if we have text, show it
						 **/
						$('.privateNoteText').slideDown('slow');
					}
				}else{
					
					$('#privateNoteForm').slideDown('slow');
					private_note.form_displayed = true;
					/**
					 *if we are showing the form we are always hiding the text
					 **/
					$('.privateNoteText').slideUp('slow');
				}
				
				
			}
							
							
			
			function getPrivateNoteText(){
				//alert('getPrivateNoteText');
				
				$.ajax({
					url: "/ajax_process.php",
					type: 'GET',
					cache: false,
					data: (
						{
							aID: '78756',
							task: 'private_note_get'
						}
					),
					dataType: "html",
					timeout: 10000,
					complete: function(){
						//alert('getPrivateNoteText complete');
						//$("#articleCommentRatingDiv .commentLoadingDiv").remove();
					},
					success: function(html){
						
						initPrivateNote(html);
						
						toggleNoteContent();
						//alert('success: private_note.text = ' + private_note.text);
						
					}
				});
			}
			
			function ajaxFormPreSubmit_privateNoteForm() {
				var alert_str = 'ajaxFormPreSubmit_privateNoteForm' + "\n";
				//alert(alert_str);
				
				var result = true;
				
				/**
				 *2009-01-04
				 *we allow them to send nothing, this would allow them to remove an existing note, but it does not delete the record
				 *if only sets the value to empty
				 *
				
				if ($('#mynotes').val() == '') {
					result = false;
					alert('You must enter text into the note section.');
				}
		 */
				
				if (result == true) {
					$('#privateNoteForm').fadeTo("slow", .3);
				}
		
				
				
				return result;
			}

			social_net_obj.links['comment'].pos_x = 0;

			social_net_obj.links['share'].use_bg_img = 1;
			*/
						
		
			$(document).ready(
				function() {
					//alert('getJavascript_socialNetworkLinks ready line: 15331');
					//console.log('getJavascript_socialNetworkLinks ready line: 15332');
					
					for(var i in social_net_obj.links){
						//console.log(social_net_obj.links[i]);
					}
					
					
					
					
					$('.articleDiv .socialNetworkLinks a').each(
						function(i){
							//alert(this.rel);
							//alert(this.rel + ' use_bg_img: ' + social_net_obj.links[this.rel].use_bg_img);
							
							/**
							 *do we want to replace the text of the link with a background image
							 */
							if(social_net_obj.links[this.rel].use_bg_img){
								$(this).html('').css(
										{
											'background-image' : 'url(http://cf2.primecp.com/images/buttons-article-page_v2.png)',
											'width' : social_net_obj.links[this.rel].width + 'px',
											'height' : social_net_obj.links[this.rel].height + 'px',
											'background-position' : social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_x + 'px ' + social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_y + 'px',
											'background-color' : 'transparent'
										}
									).hover(
										function(){
											$(this).css(
												{
													'background-position' : social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_hover_x + 'px ' + social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_y + 'px',
													'background-color' : 'transparent'
												}
											);
										},
										function(){
											$(this).css('background-position', social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_x + 'px ' + social_net_obj.links[this.rel].pos_y + 'px');
										}
									);
							}
							
							$(this).click(
								function(){
									//alert($(this).attr('id'));
									if(social_net_obj.links[this.rel].click){
										// the var stores the name of a function.
										// call it here
										return social_net_obj.links[this.rel].click($(this).attr('id'));
									}
								}
							);
							
							//alert('END ' + this.rel);
						}
					);
					
					
					
					$('.articleDiv .shareLinks .closeBtn').click(
						function(){
							$('.articleDiv .shareLinks').hide();
							
							return false;
						}
					);
					//console.log('line: 15397');
					
					
				} // end main func
			); // end ready;

				alert(alert_str);
				*/
				
				/**
				 *we are always showing the content when the btn/link is clicked

				 *the content contains its own close box
				 */
				$(share_box).css(
					{
						'left' : (btn_offset.left - ( $(share_box).width() / 2) + (btn_width / 2) ),

					}

				/**

						'left' : (btn_offset.left - ( $(share_box).width() / 2) + (btn_width / 2) ),
						'top' : (btn_offset.top + $(share_btn).height() + 2)
					}
				).toggle();
				 */
				
				return false;
			}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var realted_articles = {};
			realted_articles.main_div_obj;
			realted_articles.scroll_div_obj;
			realted_articles.left_arrow_obj;
			realted_articles.right_arrow_obj;
			
			realted_articles.num_dls = 0;
			realted_articles.dl_width = 0;
			realted_articles.dl_margin = 25;
			realted_articles.scroll_amt = 0;
			realted_articles.max_left = 0;
			
			//&lt;img class="arrow-left"
			//
			
			$(document).ready(
				function(){
					var ready_arr = [
						'FUNCTION: getJavascript_relatedArticles',
						'CLASS: TemplateContentGenerator',
					];
					var ready_str = ready_arr.join("\n\n");
					//alert(ready_str);
					//console.log(ready_str);
					
					realted_articles.init();
					
					
				}
			); // end ready_str
			
			realted_articles.init = function(){
			
				realted_articles.main_div_obj = $('#relatedArticles');
				realted_articles.scroll_div_obj = $(realted_articles.main_div_obj).find('.scrollerDiv');
				
				//var dls = $(realted_articles.main_div_obj).find('dl');
				//console.log('dls ' + dls.length);
				//console.log(dls);
				
				$(realted_articles.main_div_obj).find('dl').each(
					function(){
						realted_articles.num_dls++;
						realted_articles.dl_width = $(this).width();
					}
				)
				
				//console.log('realted_articles.num_dls ' + realted_articles.num_dls);
				//console.log('realted_articles.dl_width ' + realted_articles.dl_width);
				
				realted_articles.scroll_amt = (realted_articles.dl_width + realted_articles.dl_margin) * 4;
				
				realted_articles.max_left = (realted_articles.dl_width + realted_articles.dl_margin) * (realted_articles.num_dls - 1);
				//console.log('realted_articles.max_left ' + realted_articles.max_left);
				
				realted_articles.left_arrow_obj = $(realted_articles.main_div_obj).find('.arrow-left');
				realted_articles.right_arrow_obj = $(realted_articles.main_div_obj).find('.arrow-right');
				
				$(realted_articles.left_arrow_obj).click(
					function(){
						//console.log('click left');
						realted_articles.scroll(realted_articles.scroll_amt);
					}
				);
				
				$(realted_articles.right_arrow_obj).click(
					function(){
						//console.log('click right');
						realted_articles.scroll(-realted_articles.scroll_amt);
					}
				);
				
			}
			
			realted_articles.scroll = function(val){
				//console.log('val ' + val);
				
				var position = $(realted_articles.scroll_div_obj).position();
				var left = position.left + (val);
				if(left &gt; 0){
					//left = 0;
					left = -realted_articles.max_left + (realted_articles.dl_width + realted_articles.dl_margin);
					//$(realted_articles.left_arrow_obj).css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}else if(Math.abs(left) &gt; realted_articles.max_left){
					//console.log('too far ');
					//left = position.left;
					left = 0;
					//$(realted_articles.right_arrow_obj).css('visibility', 'hidden');
				}else{
					//$(realted_articles.left_arrow_obj).css('visibility', 'visible');
					//$(realted_articles.right_arrow_obj).css('visibility', 'visible');
				}
				
				//console.log('left ' + left);	
				//console.log('realted_articles.max_left ' + realted_articles.max_left);
				
				$(realted_articles.scroll_div_obj).animate(
					{
						'left': left + 'px'
					},
					500,
					function() {
						//console.log('Animation complete');
					}
				);
			}
  </script>

                                    }else{

				);
				
				$(user_images_dhtml.right_arrow_obj).click(
					function(){
						////console.log('click right');
						user_images_dhtml.scroll(-user_images_dhtml.scroll_amt);

				//$(user_images_dhtml.main_div_obj).find('a.rate').click(
                $(user_images_dhtml.main_div_obj).find('.rate img').click(
					function(){
    					//console.log('click rate link');
    					//console.log(user_images_dhtml.current_image_id);
    					//console.log(user_images_dhtml.ids_rated);
    					//console.log( user_images_dhtml.ids_rated.indexOf( parseInt(user_images_dhtml.current_image_id) ) );
