						}
					);
					
					yoga_slider_ad.hijackForm_editRecordForm();
					
					
				} // end main func
			); // end ready;
			
			
			yoga_slider_ad.getMainContent = function(){
			
				yoga_slider_ad.yaid = $('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' form input[name=yaid]').val();
			
				$('#' + yoga_slider_ad.main_text_id).html('');
				
				$.ajax({
					url: "/primeads/ajax_process.php",
					type: 'GET',
					cache: false,
					dataType: "html",
					timeout: 10000,
					data: (
						{
							task: 'get_main_content',
							yaID: yoga_slider_ad.yaid
						}
					),
					complete: function(){
						
					},
					success: function(html){
						$('#' + yoga_slider_ad.main_text_id).html(html);
					}
				});
			}
			
			
			yoga_slider_ad.hijackForm_editRecordForm = function(){
				//alert('yoga_slider_ad.hijackForm_editRecordForm');
				
				$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' form').ajaxForm(
					{
						beforeSubmit: yoga_slider_ad.preSubmitForm_editRecordForm,
						dataType: 'json',
						success: function(json) {
							
							/*
							*get rid of any error bg colors from previous submission
							*/
							$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' :input').css(
								{
									'background-color' : '#fff'
								}
							);
						
							if(json.result == 1){
								$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' .thanksDiv').show();						
								$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' .sliderMainContent').slideUp();
								
								
								setTimeout("$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class).slideUp()", 2000);
								
							}else{
							
								$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' .sliderMainContent').fadeTo('normal', 1.0);
								
								var num_errors = json.errors.length;
								//alert('num_errors: ' + num_errors);
								if(num_errors &gt; 0){
									for(var x=0; x&lt;num_errors; x++){
										$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' :input[name=' + json.errors[x] + ']').css(
											{
												'background-color' : '#fffcdf'
											}
										);
									}
									alert('We could not sign you up. Please see the form for errors.');
								}
							}
							
							
						}
					}
				);
			}
			
			yoga_slider_ad.preSubmitForm_editRecordForm = function(){
				//alert('yoga_slider_ad.preSubmitForm_editRecordForm');
				
				$('.' + yoga_slider_ad.wrapper_class + ' .sliderMainContent').fadeTo('normal', 0.1);
				
				return true;
			}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $.widget( "custom.catcomplete", $.ui.autocomplete, {
				_renderMenu: function( ul, items ) {
					var self = this,
						currentCategory = "";
					$.each( items, function( index, item ) {
						if ( item.category != currentCategory ) {
							ul.append( "&lt;li class='ui-autocomplete-category'&gt;" + item.category + "&lt;/li&gt;" );
							currentCategory = item.category;
						}
						self._renderItem( ul, item );
					});
				}
			});
			
			
			$(document).ready(
				function(){
					var ready_arr = [
						'FUNCTION: getJavascript_headerSearchFormAutoComplete',
						'CLASS: Search'
					];
					var ready_str = ready_arr.join("\n\n");
					//alert(ready_str);
					//console.log(ready_str);
					
					
					/* start autocomplete */
					$( "#search_term" ).autocomplete({
						source: function(request, response){
							var alert_str = 'source callback 1' + "\n\n";
							alert_str += 'request: ' + request + "\n\n";
							alert_str += 'response: ' + response + "\n\n";
							//alert(alert_str);
							//console.log(alert_str);
							
							if( 1 ){
								$.ajax(
									{
										url: "/ajax_process.php",
										dataType: "json",
										/**
										 *add additional params to the data sent to the server?
										 *request is an object. we are adding properties listed in the {}
										 */
										data: $.extend(
											{
												task: "search_autofill"
											},
											request
										),
										success: function(data) {
											//alert('autocomplete success');
											response(data);
										}
									}
								);
							}
						},
						minLength: 3,
						select: function( event, ui ){
							//alert('select a suggestion');
							//$('#headerSearchForm').submit(); // this would submit the form immediately when a &lt;li&gt; is clicked
							/**
							 *we want the selection of a suggested value to trigger the form to submit
							 *we needed to add a small delay otherwise the selected term is not passed
							 *only the orig text the user typed in is passed
							 */
							 
							// would like to see this selector / id passed to this func as a param one day 
							setTimeout("$('#headerSearchForm').submit();", 500);
						},
						close: function(event, ui){
							//alert('close');
						}
					});
					/* end autocomplete */
					
				}
			);
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var standard_header_search_obj = {};
			
			standard_header_search_obj.form_id = 'headerSearchForm';
			standard_header_search_obj.search_field_name = 'search_term';
			standard_header_search_obj.search_field_default_val = 'Search';
			
			$(document).ready(
				function(){
					
					var ready_arr = [
						'FUNCTION: getJavascript_standardHeaderSearch',
						'CLASS: Search',
						'standard_header_search_obj.form_id: ' + standard_header_search_obj.form_id,
						'standard_header_search_obj.search_field_name: ' + standard_header_search_obj.search_field_name,
						'standard_header_search_obj.search_field_default_val: ' + standard_header_search_obj.search_field_default_val,
						
					];
					var ready_str = ready_arr.join("\n\n");
					//alert(ready_str);
					//console.log(ready_str);
					
					standard_header_search_obj.init();
				}
			); // end ready
			
			
            standard_header_search_obj.init = function(){
                standard_header_search_obj.form_obj = $('#' + standard_header_search_obj.form_id);
                
				$(standard_header_search_obj.form_obj).submit(
					function(){
					    
					    //console.log('submit form');
						
						var result = true;
						
						var search_str = $(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj).val();
						//console.log('search_str: ' + search_str);
						var search_str2 = search_str.replace(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_default_val, '');
						//console.log('search_str2: ' + search_str2);
						
						$(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj).val(search_str2);
						if(search_str2 == ''){
							alert('Please enter a search term.');
							$(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj).select();
							result = false;
						}
						
						//console.log('result: ' + result);
						//return false;
						
						if(result == true){
							$(this).find('input[type=submit]').fadeTo('normal', 0.2);
						
							$(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj).addClass('waiting');
						}else{
    						// somwhere, the form get opacity 0.2 on submit (i do not know where)
    						// get the form showing again
    						$(standard_header_search_obj.form_obj).fadeTo('normal', 1.0);
						}
						
						
						return result;
					}
				);
				
				standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj = $(standard_header_search_obj.form_obj).find('input[name=' + standard_header_search_obj.search_field_name + ']');
				
				$(standard_header_search_obj.search_field_obj).click(
					function(){
						// console.log('click - ' + $(this).val() );
						
                    }
                );
				
            } // end init
  </script>

$(document).ready(
    function() {
        $('.articleResultDiv').hover(function() {
            if ($(window).width() &gt; 1024) {
                $(this).find('.slidingTitle').slideDown('slow');
                $(this).find('.slidingBottom').slideDown('slow');
            }
        }, function() {
            if ($(window).width() &gt; 1024) {
                $(this).find('.slidingTitle').slideUp('slow');
                $(this).find('.slidingBottom').slideUp('slow');
            }
        });

        $('.articleDiv .addToMyBox a').click(function() {
            if(user_logged_in){
                
                var link_parent = $(this).parents('.addToMyBox');
                //console.log('click addToMyBox');
                var aID = $(this).attr('rel');
                //console.log(aID);
                
                
                var task = 'add_article_to_box';
                if($(this).hasClass('removeFromMyBoxLink')){
                    //console.log('remove');
                    task = 'remove_article_from_box';
                }
                
                $.ajax(
            		{
            			type: "POST",
            			dataType: "json",
            			timeout: 10000,
            			url: '/ajax_process.php',
            			data: {
            				task: task,
            				aID: aID
            			},
            			success: function (json) {
            				//console.log(link_parent);
            				if(json.success == 1){
                				switch(task){
                    				case 'add_article_to_box':
                    				    $(link_parent).find('.addToMyBoxLink').hide();
                    				    $(link_parent).find('.removeFromMyBoxLink').show();
                    				    break;
                    				case 'remove_article_from_box':
                    				    $(link_parent).find('.removeFromMyBoxLink').hide();
                    				    $(link_parent).find('.addToMyBoxLink').show();
                    				    break;    
                				}
            				}
            			},
            			error: function (XMLHttpRequest, textStatus, errorThrown) {
            				//alert('There was an error getting the data for the article.');
            			},
            			complete: function () {
            				
            			}
            		}
            	);
                
                
            }else{
                login_dhtml_obj.displayLoginDhtmlBox('dhtmlLogin', 'You must login to add items to your list.');
            }
            
        });
        
        
		
		
		
		$('#search_term').click(
			function () {
				//console.log('search_term');
				if ($(this).hasClass('defaultSearchText')) {
					// remove the class that sets the text color to grey
					$(this).removeClass('defaultSearchText');
					// remove the default text
					$(this).val('');
				}
				
			}
		);
		
		
		//checkNlSignUpCookie();
		
		
		// set the onclick of the newsletter sign up email text field
		$('#newsletterSignUpForm #email').click( 
			function () {
				// this removes the default text that appears in the text field
				$('#newsletterSignUpForm #email').val('');	
				
				if ($(this).hasClass('defaultTextFieldColor')) {
					// remove the class that sets the text color to grey
					$(this).removeClass('defaultTextFieldColor');
					// remove the default text
					$(this).val('');
				}
			}
			
		);
		
		
		// newsletter signup form - right column
		$('#newsletterSignUpForm').ajaxForm(
			{
				beforeSubmit: ajaxFormPreSubmit,
				success: function(response) {
				
				    post_newsletter_signup.criteo = response.criteo;
				
					// log all submits, passing something about the success/new user
					post_newsletter_signup.logRightRailSubmit(response.is_new_signup, $('#newsletterSignUpForm :input[name=rriID]').val());
					
					
					//alert('result = ' + response.result);
					
					$('#newsletterSignUpLoader').hide();
					
					if (response.result &gt; 0) {
						
						// the user is signed up
						
						//triggerWiderFunnel();
						
						// hide the sign up form fields
						$('#newsletterSignUpForm').hide();
						
						// display thanks
						$('#newsletterSignUpThanks').show();

						alert_str += 'COOKIE_EXP_DAYS_NL_SIGNUP = 1825' + "\n";
						//alert(alert_str);
						createCookie('nlsignup', 1825, 1825);
						
						
						signup_redirect_qry_params['email'] = response.email;
						signup_redirect_qry_params['enc_email'] = response.enc_email;
						
						
						
						
						
						post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup = response.is_new_signup; // right rail
						postNewsletterSignup();
						
					} else {
						// display error
						//alert('response.result = ' + response.result);
						
						$('#newsletterSignUpError').show();
						setTimeout("$('#newsletterSignUpError').hide()", 5000);
						
						$('#newsletterSignUpForm').fadeTo("slow", 1);

						$("#lname").attr("disabled", false);
						$("#email").attr("disabled", false);
						$("#signUpSubmit").attr("disabled", false);
						
						//alert('Sorry, we could not sign you up.');
					}
					
					
	
					
					
					
					
					
					//alert('newsletterSignUpForm success ' + response.lname);
					
					//alert($("#lname").attr("disabled"););

			}
		);

function displayDhtmlPrivacyPolicy(){
	//alert('newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink a click');
				//return false;
				
				// hide the link that opened the privacy
				$("#newsletterSignUpPrivacyLink").hide();
				
				// hide the link that closes the dhtml content
				$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnimeCloseLink").hide();
				
				
				
				// jump to the top of the page
				window.location = '#';
				
				// fade out the signup form content
				$('#newsletterSignUpAnimeContent').fadeTo('slow', 0.3);
				
				
				// get 80% the height of the browser window
				var win_height = $(window).height() * .8;
				
				// show the privacy policy
				$('#newsletterSignUpPrivacyContent').height(win_height).show();
				
				
				
				
				
				
				return false;
}

2014-03-28

function checkNlSignUpCookie() {
	
	//alert('checkNlSignUpCookie');
	
	var the_cookie = readCookie('nlsignup');
	
	if (the_cookie) {
		// the user has the cookie
		// do not do anything
	} else {
		
		//alert('call displayDhtmlSignup from checkNlSignUpCookie');
		displayDhtmlSignup();

	}
	
}


//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

/*
2014-03-28
dont think is is called anymore, but not much evidence to support that
*/

function clickToSubscribe() {
	
	// look at the cookie
	var the_cookie = readCookie('nlsignup');
	
	// if present
	if (the_cookie) {
		// get rid of the cookie and reload the current page
		eraseCookie('nlsignup');
		window.location.reload();
	} else {
		// call func to show signup
		displayDhtmlSignup();
		
	}
	
}

//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function displayDhtmlSignup() {
	
	//alert('displayDhtmlSignup');
	
	animateDhtmlSignup();
	
}

//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function animateDhtmlSignup(){
	//console.log('animateDhtmlSignup (line 1279)');
	
	
	
	
	/*
	2014-03-28
	there seem to be a lot of ways this gets called, and i dont pretend to know them all
	so we are adding the nscID test here
	*/
	if(nscID == false){
		//console.log('no dhtml create to show');
		return false;
	}
	
	// move user to top of the page
	//window.location = '#';
	
	var doc_width = $(document).width();
	var doc_height = $(document).height();

	var popup_width = $("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").width();
	
	var popup_left = 0;
	if (popup_width &lt; doc_width) {
		popup_left = (doc_width - popup_width) / 2;
	}
		
	$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").css("top", '-600px');
	$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").css("left", popup_left + 'px');
	$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").show();
	
	//console.log('call animation (line 1311)');
	
	$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").animate(
		{"top": "10px"}, 
		"slow",
		'',
		function () {
    		
    		console.log( 'newsletterSignUpDivAnime animate done' );
            
			// this fires after the popup is in place
			// fade out the div that will be placed over the page
			// the div is not visible at this point, but we use fade out so we can fade it in after the css updates are made
			
			$('#viewportGreyout').fadeTo(
				"fast", 
				0.0,
				function () {
					
					// set some css for the div then fade it in
					$('#viewportGreyout').css(
						{
							position: 'absolute',
							margin: 0,
							padding: 0,
							'z-index': 500,
							'top' : '0',
							'left' : '0',
							'width' : doc_width + 'px',
							'height' : doc_height + 'px',
							'background-color' : '#000'
						}
					).fadeTo("slow", 0.8).click(
					    function(){
					        /*
					        2014-06-23
					        clicking the greyout closes the dhtml, as if you clicked the close link/button
					        */
    					    //console.log('click the greyport');
    					    //console.log('desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout: ' + desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout);
    					    if(desktop_dhtml_newsletter_signup_obj.click_closes_greyout &gt; 0){
        					    $("#newsletterSignUpDivAnimeCloseLink").click();
    					    }
					    }
					);
				}
			);
		}
	);
	
	//console.log('animateDhtmlSignup END (line 1361)');

} // end animateDhtmlSignup

function hideNewsletterSignUpFormAnime() {
	/**
	 *move the dhtml up off the page
	 */
	$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").animate(
		{"top": "-1000px"}, 
		"slow",
		function () {
			/**
			 *hide the grey out div
			 */
			$('#viewportGreyout').css(
				{
					'width' : '0px',
					'height' : '0px',
					'background-color' : 'transparent'
				}
			).fadeTo("fast",0.0);
			
			/**
			 *remove the signup html from the dom
			 *saves memory?
			 *prevents the content from printing
			 */
			$("#newsletterSignUpDivAnime").remove();
		}
	);
}



//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function signupRedirect() {
	
	/*if (is_mustang == 1) {
		alert('signupRedirect signup_redirect_url = ' + signup_redirect_url);
	}*/
	
	
	
	// do we have a redirect url
	if (signup_redirect_url != '') {
		
		
		// set some vars that are strings we will search for
		var replace_site_url = '[site_url]';
		var replace_email = '[email]';
		var replace_enc_email = '[e]';
		
		// go through each string, if it is not empty
		if (replace_site_url != '') {
			// add the home page url for this site, urlencoded
			signup_redirect_url = signup_redirect_url.replace(replace_site_url, escape('http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com'));
		}
		
		if (replace_email != '') {
			// add the email address the user signed up with
			signup_redirect_url = signup_redirect_url.replace(replace_email, signup_redirect_qry_params['email']);
		}
	
        if (replace_enc_email != '') {
			// add the email address the user signed up with
			signup_redirect_url = signup_redirect_url.replace(replace_enc_email, signup_redirect_qry_params['enc_email']);
		}		
		
				if(post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup == true){
			var addl_qry_str = '?';
			if(signup_redirect_url.indexOf("?") &gt; 0){
				// the url already has a query string, so just tack on to it
				addl_qry_str = '&amp;';
			}
			
			signup_redirect_url += addl_qry_str + 'pp=1';
		}
		
		
				
		if (is_mustang == 1) {
			var confirm_str = 'signupRedirect' + "\n\n";
			confirm_str += 'replace_site_url = ' + replace_site_url + "\n\n";
			confirm_str += 'replace_email = ' + replace_email + "\n\n";
			confirm_str += 'post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup = ' + post_newsletter_signup.is_new_signup + "\n\n";
			
			confirm_str += 'signup_redirect_qry_params[email] = ' + signup_redirect_qry_params['enc_email'] + "\n\n\n\n";
			
			confirm_str += 'signup_redirect_url = ' + signup_redirect_url + "\n\n";
			confirm_str += 'http_host = http://www.allfreecrochetafghanpatterns.com' + "\n\n";
			
			confirm_str += 'signup_redirect_id = ' + signup_redirect_id + "\n\n";
			
			confirm_str += 'Click OK to stay on this page.' + "\n";
			confirm_str += 'Click Cancel to go to Flow URL.' + "\n";
			
			if (confirm(confirm_str)) {
				return;
			}
		}
		
		// redirect the user
		window.location = signup_redirect_url;
		
		
		
	}
	
	
}
						
//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

function postNewsletterSignup() {
    console.log('postNewsletterSignup');
	/*
	2014-04-08
	we do more post signup stuff, so we want to delay always (at least I think always)
	*/
	
	console.log('display_sub_center_post_signup: ' + display_sub_center_post_signup);
	
		
	/*
	2014-04-08
	record which flow we sent the user to
	we test if it is greater than 0
	when we have no set flow, the code will set the flow url to /, and the id gets set to 0
	we are not logging that
	*/
	if(signup_redirect_id &gt; 0){
		// we do not need a response for the ajax call logFlowID, but we are still giving a small delay
		post_newsletter_signup.logFlowID(signup_redirect_id);
	}
	
	if(display_sub_center_post_signup == 1){
    	if(dhtmlSubCenter != undefined  &amp;&amp;  dhtmlSubCenter.trigger != undefined){
        	hideNewsletterSignUpFormAnime();
        	dhtmlSubCenter.email = dhtml_sub_center_email;
        	dhtmlSubCenter.trigger();
        	
        	return;
    	}
	}
	
	// this only runs if dhtmlSubCenter.trigger() not called
    signupRedirect();
	
} // end postNewsletterSignup

/**
 *additional widder funnel js might be on the page / included in the html
 *if it is, the WFpageTracker var is likely an object (barring errors)
 *otherwise, this will get called harmlessly
 */
function triggerWiderFunnel(){
	var alert_str = 'call to triggerWiderFunnel' + "\n";
	//alert(alert_str);
	
	//WIDERFUNNEL GWO GOAL CALL
	if(typeof(WFpageTracker)==='object'){
		wf_goal();
		
		alert_str += 'WFpageTracker IS an object' + "\n";
	}else{
		alert_str += 'WFpageTracker IS NOT an object' + "\n";
		alert_str += 'typeof(WFpageTracker): ' + typeof(WFpageTracker) + "\n";
	}
	
	if (is_mustang == 1) {
		alert(alert_str);
	}
	
}

post_newsletter_signup.logRightRailSubmit = function(isNewSignup, rriID){
	//console.log('post_newsletter_signup.logRightRailSubmit');
	//console.log('is_new_signup: ' + is_new_signup);
	//console.log('rriID: ' + rriID);
	
	if(isNewSignup == 1 || isNewSignup == true){
		isNewSignup = 1;
	}else{
		isNewSignup = 0;
	}
	
	$.ajax(
		{
			type: "POST",
			dataType: "json",
			timeout: '10000',
			url: "/ajax_process.php",
			data: {
				task: 'log_right_rail_submit',
				rriID: rriID,
				isNewSignup: isNewSignup
			},
			success: function(json) {
		     	
			}
		}
	);
}

			url: "/ajax_process.php",
			data: {
				task: 'log_flow_id',
				fuID: signup_redirect_id
			},
			success: function(json) {
			
			}
		}
	);
}
